      <DBImportSourceSql>select *,StoreCount+BranchAllStoreCount as ALLStoreCount,AverageDaily*7 as AverageWeekly,AverageDaily*15 as Average15,AverageDaily*30 as Average30,#@PurchaseCount#
from (select SPBMZD.ZZSL as DrugPoint
,SPBMZD.LSJ as DrugPriceRetail
,SPBMZD.lsj1 as DrugPriceWholeSale
,SPBMZD.ZDXJ as DrugPriceLowest
,#@StoreLowerrLimit# as StoreLowerrLimit
,#@StoreUpperLimit# as StoreUpperLimit
,SPBMZD.ID as DrugSerialNo
,SPBMZD.HH AS DrugArtNo 
,(SELECT  isnull(SUM(SL) / 90,0) AS sl FROM fgs_xsd where hh=SPBMZD.HH and KDRQ&gt;(DATEADD(day, - 90, GETDATE()))) as AverageDaily
,(ceiling(isnull(xs1.sl,0)*0.3+isnull(xs2.sl,0)*0.2+isnull(xs3.sl,0)*0.5)) as AverageMonthly
,isnull(SPBMZD.SJSL,0) AS StoreCount
,SPBMZD.BZSL AS 基本信息补货线  
,SPBMZD.JJ1 AS 最低进价
,SPBMZD.JJ AS 上次进价
,SPBMZD.GG as Specification
,SPBMZD.CD as ProductionAddress
,SPBMZD.JX as DosageForm
,SPBMZD.LDW as Unit
,isnull((select sum(sjsl) FROM fgs_spbmzd where HH=SPBMZD.HH),0) as BranchAllStoreCount
,CGJHSP.KCBHX AS StorePurchaseLine
,CGJHSP.KCSKCX AS 锁库存线
,CGJHSP.CYCLEDAYS AS 采购周期
,isnull(CSGYS.DHTS,0) AS 在途天数
,isnull((select sum(isnull(SL,0)-isnull(DHSL,0)) from fgs_CGJHD where hh=SPBMZD.hh and JZBZ=1 and DJZT&lt;2),0) AS 门店计划未达成
,(isnull((select sum(sjsl) from v_ywbalance_kxs kxs where kxs.SPID=SPBMZD.ID),0)/(ceiling(isnull(xs1.sl,0)*0.3+isnull(xs2.sl,0)*0.2+isnull(xs3.sl,0)*0.5))) AS 存销比
,SPBMZD.ZBZ as 中包装
,SPBMZD.MJL as 每件量
,isnull((SELECT  top 1 SUM(isnull(SL,0))-SUM(isnull(DHSL,0)) as sl FROM CGDD WHERE DDZT&lt;&gt;3  and jzbz&lt;&gt;0 and HH=SPBMZD.HH
	      -- AND KDRQ &gt;=DATEADD(DAY,-7,GETDATE())  
GROUP BY HH having SUM(ISNULL(SL,0)) &gt;SUM(ISNULL(DHSL,0))),0) as TransportingCount
,isnull((select sum(sl) from  fgs_cgjhd where  KDRQ&gt; DATEADD(day, - 10, GETDATE()) and hh=SPBMZD.HH),0) as StoresPlanNumber
,cast(SPBMZD.tgbz  as  bit) StopPurchase
,#@BranchPlanNumber# as 门店计划数量
,(select isnull(sum(sl),0) from fgs_JZDBD where KDRQ &gt;DATEADD(DAY,-30,getdate()) and hh=SPBMZD.HH) as 月调拨量
,(select isnull(sum(sl),0) from fgs_JZDBD where KDRQ &gt;DATEADD(DAY,-30,getdate()) and hh=010001 and DRFGSID in (select id from CSKHZD where zy&lt;&gt;'1' and  KHLX=2)) as 加盟店月调拨量
FROM CSSPBMZD  SPBMZD 
LEFT JOIN CGJHSP ON CGJHSP.HH = SPBMZD.HH
LEFT JOIN CSGYS  on SPBMZD.JHDW=CSGYS.DWBH
left join 
(select spid,sum(sl)/3 sl from fgs_xsd where 
kdrq between  dateadd(day,-90,convert(date,getdate())) 
and  convert(date,getdate())
group by spid)xs1 on spbmzd.id=xs1.spid
left join 
(select spid,sum(sl) sl from fgs_xsd where 
kdrq between  dateadd(MONTH,-12,convert(date,getdate())) 
and  dateadd(MONTH,-11,convert(date,getdate()))
group by spid)xs2 on spbmzd.id=xs2.spid
left join 
(select spid,sum(sl) sl from fgs_xsd where 
kdrq between  dateadd(day,-30,convert(date,getdate())) 
and  convert(date,getdate())
group by spid)xs3 on spbmzd.id=xs3.spid
where SPBMZD.hh in (#@DrugNoList#)
) t  where #@PlanRuleContent# </DBImportSourceSql>

      <DBGetLotNumSql>SELECT phk.PH,phk.XQ,SUM(phk.SL - ISNULL(skc.skcsl,0))  AS SL ,CSSPBMZD.ID AS DrugSerialNo,CSSPBMZD.HH AS DrugSerialNo,ck.NAME as CKName,g.MC ,PHK.JHDJ
                            FROM  PHK 
				      INNER JOIN  CSSPBMZD ON phk.hh = CSSPBMZD.HH
				       LEFT JOIN  (SELECT pcid, SUM(sl) AS skcsl FROM dbo.fgs_SKC WHERE fgsid = 0 AND pcid &gt; 0   GROUP BY pcid ) skc ON dbo.PHK.id = skc.pcid 
					   left join CSCKBM ck on phk.CKBH = ck.ID
					   inner join CSGYS g on g.DWBH=PHK.JHDW
				           WHERE  SL &gt; 0 and CSSPBMZD.HH='#@DrugArtNo#'
				        GROUP BY  CSSPBMZD.ID  ,phk.PH  ,phk.XQ ,CSSPBMZD.HH ,PHK.CKBH,PHK.ID ,ck.NAME,g.MC ,PHK.JHDJ
